Abstract: Recent breakthroughs in 3D generation have advanced notably with the development of text-to-image diffusion model. However, existing methods remain two practical challenges: (1) They primarily generate single 3D object, but struggle to generate multi-object compositional 3D assets due to the lack of the modeling for Gaussian primitives in reasonable interactions. (2) They often suffer from cross-view inconsistency during 3D optimization, as Score Distillation Sampling inherently performs on each single view, inevitably resulting in cross-view hallucinations. To solve above issues, we propose I2C-3D, a novel optimization-based method to generate multi-view consistent compositional 3D assets with reasonable interactions. Specifically, we propose an Inclusive Interactive Collisions strategy to guide Gaussian primitives appearing in reasonable interaction regions naturally, thereby ensuring objects in the compositional scene interact in a physically plausible and visually coherent way. Additionally, to enhance multi-view consistency, Multi-View Adaptive Score Distillation Sampling is devised to distill multi-view consistency prior and layout prior from pre-trained diffusion model by modulating attention map of instance token and spatial token across viewpoints. Benefiting from above elaborate designs, I2C-3D not only generates high-fidelity multi-view consistent compositional 3D assets but also supports 3D editing flexibly, facilitating complex scene generation. Extensive experiments demonstrate our I2C-3D outperforms existing methods in generation quality and multi-view consistency.

Abstract: Accurate pulmonary vessel segmentation remains challenging due to the sparse, tortuous, and multi-scale nature of vascular structures, where small branches are easily lost and topology integrity is difficult to preserve under voxel-wise supervision. Existing deep segmentation models primarily optimize binary masks, lacking explicit geometric constraints, thus struggling to recover continuous tubular morphology and fine vascular connectivity. In this study, we introduce MorVess, a morphology-aware segmentation framework that integrates differentiable geometric priors with large-scale foundation model adaptation to achieve fine-grained vascular parsing. Our source code is available at https://github.com/MaoFuyou/MorVess.

### [42] [Geometry-Instructed Video Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24225)
*Chirui Chang,Xiaoyang Lyu,Yi-Hua Huang,Haoru Tan,Shizhen Zhao,Yikang Ding,Jianmin Bao,Xin Tao,Pengfei Wan,Xiaojuan Qi*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: GIVE提出以统一“对象状态”表征驱动的几何指令视频编辑，通过成对的几何流（深度框+朝向框）精确指定编辑前后对象的3D状态，实现平移/旋转/缩放/复制/删除等操作，并保持阴影、反射等次生效应一致。基于可扩展图形引擎生成大规模前后成对监督数据，模型在合成与真实视频上均表现出时间一致与效果可信。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统DCC中常见的对象级几何编辑在生成式视频编辑里仍不可靠。核心难点是：跨视角与时间不歧义地描述目标对象的3D状态变化，并在编辑中自洽地更新依赖几何的次生效应（阴影、反射等）。现有方法缺少统一、紧凑且与外观无关的几何指令表示与配套数据。

Method: 提出GIVE框架：用两条与视频对齐的几何流对目标对象编辑前后状态进行统一表征——(1) depth-box编码粗3D位置与范围；(2) orientation-box提供与外观无关的朝向线索。将编辑描述为对象状态从“前”到“后”的转换。为监督学习，构建可扩展图形引擎流水线，执行对象级编辑程序，渲染严格配对的前/后视频，确保只改变期望的几何因素并使次生效应与变换一致。

Result: 在多种几何操作（平移、旋转、缩放、复制、删除）上，GIVE实现高保真几何编辑、时间一致性和阴影/反射等次生效应一致；在统一框架下优于或匹配现有方法，并可迁移到野外视频，展示良好泛化。

Conclusion: 通过统一的对象状态表示与成对监督数据，GIVE将几何编辑从传统DCC可靠性带入生成式视频编辑，兼顾时序一致与次生效应一致，为通用对象级视频几何编辑提供了可扩展方案。

Abstract: Object-level geometric edits, including translating, rotating, scaling, duplicating, or removing an object, are routine operations in digital content creation (DCC) workflows, yet they remain unreliable in generative video editing. The key challenge lies in specifying the target object's 3D state change unambiguously across viewpoint and time, while consistently updating geometry-dependent secondary effects such as shadows and reflections. We introduce GIVE, a geometry-instructed video editing framework that represents edits through a unified object-state formulation. Two video-aligned geometry streams describe the target object before and after editing: a depth-box encoding coarse 3D placement and extent, and an orientation-box providing an appearance-agnostic orientation cue. Together, these streams provide a compact pre/post geometric specification for object-state transitions. To provide paired supervision for learning these edits, we build a scalable graphics-engine pipeline that executes object-level edit programs and renders controlled before/after pairs, isolating the intended geometric edit while keeping secondary effects consistent with the transformation. Experimental results demonstrate that GIVE produces faithful geometric edits with temporal coherence and consistent secondary effects across operators in a unified framework, and shows promising transfer to in-the-wild videos. Project page: https://geometry-instructed-video-editing.github.io/give/

Abstract: The integration of visual evidence has significantly enhanced the capabilities of large multimodal models. To overcome these limitations, we propose {EVA} (LatEnt Visual StAtes), a novel framework that natively generates continuous latent visual representations. This co-optimization, notably, causes extreme policy deviation in the 'transition window' following the Latent\_slot tokens. Existing VPR methods, designed primarily for urban or indoor scenes, fail to generalize reliably across these starkly different scenarios. To address this, we propose ProteusVPR, a two-stage retrieval-refinement framework. The first stage employs any standard VPR model for initial image retrieval. The second stage introduces a geometric-visual estimation network that fuses the retrieved image with two temporally preceding frames, incorporating geometric descriptors, a local affine coordinate system, and camera azimuth encoding to achieve precise localization. To support this task, we introduce the XHZ dataset, an 8K-panoramic ship-borne dataset collected from an operational vessel, featuring multi-floor cabin structures, deck transition zones, and strict query-database separation for rigorous evaluation. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 事件相机在高时域分辨率与宽动态范围场景优势明显，但事件数据稀疏、语义弱，导致与帧式检测存在显著性能差距。现有蒸馏方法多仅关注空间语义或成对关系，难以应对复杂场景与跨模态差异。

Method: 构建M^2C-EvDet跨模态蒸馏框架：1) 频域学习+自适应频率解耦的AF^2D^2模块，对教师（帧）与学生（事件）特征在不同频段进行选择性对齐与加权蒸馏；2) 基于超图计算的MORD模块，建模多阶（高于二元）实例/区域关系，进行关系结构蒸馏。整体以帧式检测器为教师、事件检测器为学生，联合优化。

Result: 相较以往仅空间或成对关系蒸馏的方法，本框架在复杂场景下显著缩小EvDet与帧式检测的性能差距，并在多项基准上取得更优检测精度与鲁棒性（文摘层面未给出具体数值）。

Conclusion: 多域（频域+空间）与多阶（高阶关系）联合蒸馏能有效弥合事件与帧数据的跨模态差异，提升EvDet的语义表达与检测性能；AF^2D^2与MORD是关键组件。

Abstract: Event-based object Detection (EvDet), as a biologically inspired visual perception paradigm, demonstrates superior performance in scenarios demanding high temporal resolution and a wide dynamic range. Nevertheless, the inherent sparse representations and inadequate visual semantics of event data result in a considerable performance disparity between EvDet and frame-based object detection. Previous works attempt to alleviate this cross-modal discrepancy through knowledge distillation, yet they only focus on spatial visual semantics or pair-wise relational information, thus limiting performance in more complex scenarios. To address this challenge, this paper proposes M^2C-EvDet, a Multi-domain and Multi-order Cross-modal knowledge distillation framework for EvDet. Built upon frequency learning and hypergraph computation, M^2C-EvDet integrates two specialized modules: Adaptive Frequency-Decoupled Feature Distillation (AF^2D^2) and Multi-Order Relational Distillation (MORD).

### [47] [TuringViT: Making SOTA Vision Transformers Accessible to All](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24253)
*Qiman Wu,Hanlin Chen,Lyujie Chen,Rui Xin,Jianlei Zheng,Mingyuan Wang,Jiahui Hu,Da Zhu,Yuecheng Ma,Yuhua Wei,Yizhao Wang,Hua Zhou,Yuheng Zhang,Anhua Liu,Shaman Tang,Yue He,Pengfei Diao,Shuang Su,Haotong Xin,Weichao Huang,Hang Zhang,Xianming Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: TuringViT提出高效注意力TLA、监督丰富的数据策划VISTA和原生动态分辨率预训练，以更少数据训练可定制的SOTA级ViT，在高分辨率延迟、VLM集成与下游性能上超越现有开源基线，并具备良好扩展规律与易部署性。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 三项核心设计：1) Turing Linear Attention（TLA）：线性复杂度的序列建模替代softmax注意力，提升高/动态分辨率训练与推理效率；2) VISTA-Curation：构建监督信号丰富的图像-视频训练集，支持高质量多样监督；3) 原生动态分辨率预训练：从训练之初即支持可变输入分辨率，便于无缝迁移至下游VLM与多场景部署。并进行扩展规律分析与实证评测。

Result: 用仅10%数据超越领先开源ViT基线；在下游VLM任务上性能更强；高分辨率输入下延迟随分辨率扩展更优；扩展规律显示随策划数据规模增长仍稳步提升，远未饱和；实现快速适配、硬件友好与高效部署，被用作小鹏多AI系统的统一视觉基础。

Conclusion: TuringViT通过高效注意力、优质数据策划与原生动态分辨率训练，显著降低SOTA级ViT训练与定制的成本与门槛，提供可复现管线，促进社区更广泛地训练、定制与部署高性能视觉Transformer。

Abstract: Modern VLMs and VLA systems commonly adopt off-the-shelf ViTs such as SigLIP2 as visual encoders, but diverse downstream requirements in latency, temporal modeling, and VLM integration often call for customized SOTA-level ViTs. Training such encoders remains beyond the reach of much of the community, as it requires massive image-text data, while standard softmax attention makes high-resolution or dynamic-resolution pretraining prohibitively costly and often forces low-resolution pretraining followed by post-hoc adaptation. TuringViT addresses these challenges with three key designs: Turing Linear Attention (TLA) for efficient sequence modeling, VISTA-Curation to construct supervision-rich image-video training data, and native dynamic-resolution pretraining that supports flexible inputs from the start and transfers seamlessly to downstream VLMs. As a result, TuringViT outperforms leading open-source ViT baselines with only 10% of the data, achieves stronger downstream VLM performance, and delivers substantially better latency scaling on high-resolution inputs. Our scaling-law analysis further shows that TuringViT continues to improve predictably with curated data scale, far from saturation. Its fast adaptation, hardware-friendly design, and efficient deployment have made it a unified visual foundation across XPeng's AI systems. More broadly, TuringViT provides a reproducible pipeline that dramatically lowers the cost for the community to train, customize, and deploy SOTA-level ViTs, moving toward making such Vision Transformers accessible to all.

### [48] [Social Structure Matters in 3D Human-Human Interaction Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24255)
*Zhongju Wang,Beier Wang,Yatao Bian,Pichao Wang,Zhi Wang,Daoyi Dong,Hongdong Li,Huadong Mo,Zhenhong Sun*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出“Solo-to-Social”框架，用LLM规划社交结构、用运动技能模型执行，实现文本驱动的两人3D互动动作，显著提升阶段一致性、角色对齐与伙伴协调。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文本到动作方法擅长单人，但难以扩展到两人互动，因为互动需要显式/隐式的社交结构：阶段推进、角色分配、相互协同与物理可行性。作者想弄清LLM在这类结构化任务中的边界，并设计能把社交结构落地为真实运动的生成系统。

Method: 提出“规划-执行”范式：Think with LLM, Move with Motion Skill。1) 规划器：用LLM把交互语义转为与动作对齐的社会监督，包括分解阶段、分配伙伴感知的角色、并与时间序列对齐。2) 执行器：在预训练的单人动作模型上进行社会化适配，通过LoRA微调、上一阶段的自条件、以及自我坐标系下的伙伴条件输入，将规划的结构落实为两人协调的三维动作。

Result: 与基线相比，生成的两人3D互动在阶段一致性、角色对齐和伙伴协调方面更好，动作更连贯、物理更合理、对互动更敏感。

Conclusion: LLM能“思考”出社交结构但不能直接生成可行的动作；将LLM用于结构规划、再由运动模型执行的Solo-to-Social框架，有效弥合社交组织与运动实现之间的鸿沟，推动文本驱动的人-人交互生成。

Abstract: Although text-to-motion generation has achieved strong progress in synthesizing realistic single-person motions from language, extending it to text-driven 3D human-human interaction (HHI) remains non-trivial, as HHI requires modeling the underlying \textbf{social structure} that governs phase progression, actor roles, and inter-actor coordination. In this paper, we formulate HHI generation as a social structure modeling and grounding problem: the model must first infer how an interaction unfolds and how the two actors coordinate their roles, and then realize this structure as continuous, physically plausible, and partner-aware 3D motion. To study how such structure should be modeled, we first examine the capability boundary of large language models (LLMs) for HHI generation. Our analysis shows that LLMs can \textit{think} by recovering phase decompositions and partner-aware roles, but cannot directly \textit{move}, as they fail to generate dynamic, physically plausible, and interaction-aware motion. This motivates our planner-executor paradigm, \textbf{Think with LLM, Move with Motion Skill}. The LLM planner converts implicit interaction semantics into motion-aligned social supervision by decomposing interactions into phases, assigning partner-aware actor roles, and aligning them with motion sequence. The motion executor then grounds the planned social structure into coordinated two-person motion by adapting a pretrained solo motion model with LoRA, previous-phase self-conditioning, and ego-relative partner conditioning. Together, our Solo-to-Social framework bridges social organization and motion realization, producing 3D HHI with improved phase consistency, role alignment, and partner-aware coordination.

### [49] [Trimming the Long-Tail of Visual World Modeling Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24256)
*Bingxuan Li,Yining Hong,Cheng Qian,Hyeonjeong Ha,Jiateng Liu,Zhenhailong Wang,Yue Guo,Yunzhu Li,Heng Ji*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出Tailor-Bench，用于评测视觉世界模型在“长尾”物理交互（罕见/不规则）的模拟能力，并发现模型对非常见情境泛化不足，图像与视频模型在状态变化与时序一致性上均存在缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有图像/视频生成模型在常见物理交互上逼真，但主要拟合频繁样式，缺乏对物理原理的内化与可泛化能力。需要一个系统化基准来检验模型在不常见、非常规甚至违反物理属性约束的情景下能否正确推理与生成。

Method: 构建Tailor-Bench，包含三种逐步加难的场景模式：Regular（常见工具-任务配对）、Unconventional（用属性兼容的非常规替代工具测试可供性泛化）、Impossible（属性违背的工具检验约束意识）。并设定统一评测协议下的两种生成设置：Predictive（无提示预测结果）与Descriptive（给定目标结果进行忠实实现）。通过对多种图像/视频世界模型进行系统实验与误差分析评估其表现。

Result: 在从Regular到Unconventional再到Impossible的场景中，模型性能明显下降，表现出“长尾缺口”。图像模型常无法正确呈现物体状态变化；视频模型在此基础上还出现明显的时间不一致和因果连贯性问题。

Conclusion: 当前视觉世界模型对物理原则的内化与泛化有限，主要依赖表层视觉模式，难以处理非常规与违背属性约束的交互。Tailor-Bench为衡量和推动在长尾物理交互上的推理与生成能力提供了有力基准。

Abstract: Physical interactions follow a long-tailed distribution: a set of common and regular interactions dominates human experience and visual data, while a broad spectrum of rare and irregular interactions remains underrepresented. Although recent visual world models, including image and video generation models, achieve impressive realism on existing benchmarks, they primarily focus on simulating common physical interactions. This raises a central question: Do current visual world models internalize and generalize physical principles? In this work, we introduce Tailor-Bench, a benchmark that challenges world models to simulate irregular physical interactions. To enable systematic evaluation, we design three scenario modes that progressively challenge model reasoning: Regular scenarios reflect common tool-task pairs, Unconventional scenarios replace conventional tools with attribute-compatible substitutes to test affordance generalization, and Impossible scenarios introduce attribute-violating tools to probe constraint awareness. Additionally, we design two complementary settings under a unified evaluation protocol: predictive generation requires inferring outcomes without guidance, while descriptive generation specifies the target outcome for faithful realization. Our experimental results reveal a clear long-tail gap in physical world modeling: performance degrades from Regular to Unconventional and Impossible scenarios, indicating limited generalization beyond common interactions. Failure analysis further shows that models rely on superficial visual patterns: image models fail to realize correct state changes, while video models further suffer from temporal inconsistencies.

### [50] [3DCarGen: Scalable 3D Car Generation via 3D-consistent Multi-view Synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24257)
*Hongli Xiao,Youjian Zhang,Yaohui Jin,Xiaoguang Ren,Wenjing Yang,Long Lan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 3DCarGen提出面向真实场景的单视图到高保真3D汽车生成框架：先固定视角合成、经GS重建得粗3D、以此为显式先验驱动多视角扩散生成任意视角一致图，再用快速网格重建与颜色-法线联合优化恢复细节；在合成与真实数据上具更强几何一致性与重建保真度。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 输入单张图像，先从一组固定相机位合成多视图；2) 将这些视图输入前馈重建模型，基于3D Gaussian Splatting得到粗3D；3) 以显式3D先验作为条件，采用多视图扩散模型从任意相机位生成3D一致的图像；4) 在快速网格重建基础上，引入颜色-法线联合优化，从稠密合成视图恢复细致且连贯的3D车模。

Result: 在合成与真实数据集上，相较现有方法，3DCarGen展现出更稳健的跨视图几何一致性和更高的重建保真度；能从单张真实图像生成高质量、可控、稠密多视角并恢复精细网格。

Conclusion: 将显式3D先验与多视图扩散结合，并辅以高效网格与联合优化，可从单图扩展到任意视角、提高几何一致性与保真度，适用于真实场景的高质量3D车辆资产生成；代码与模型将开源。

Abstract: High-quality 3D vehicle assets are essential for autonomous driving simulation. Although multi-view diffusion-based paradigms enable controllable single-image reconstruction, they typically produce limited viewpoints and exhibit cross-view geometric inconsistencies, thereby reducing reconstruction fidelity in real-world scenarios. In this work, we introduce 3DCarGen, a scalable single-view 3D car generation framework designed for real-world images by synthesizing an arbitrary number of 3D-consistent multi-view images. Specifically, given a single image as input, we first synthesize a set of images from fixed viewpoints. These images are then fed into a feed-forward reconstruction model, resulting in a coarse 3D representation based on 3D Gaussian Splatting. Conditioned on this explicit 3D prior, our multi-view diffusion model generates 3D-consistent images from arbitrary camera viewpoints. We further extend a fast mesh reconstruction algorithm by incorporating color-normal joint optimization to recover detailed and coherent 3D vehicle models from the synthesized dense views. Extensive experiments on synthetic and real-world datasets demonstrate that our approach achieves robust geometric consistency and reconstruction fidelity compared to existing methods. Code and models will be released.

### [51] [MotifGen: Spatiotemporal interpolation of misaligned satellite images via multi-source generative modeling, in an application to tropical cyclones](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24263)
*Clément Dauvilliers,Claire Monteleoni*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出首个可处理多源、非均匀时空采样的生成式模型，用于热带气旋微波图像插值；自监督遮盖重建训练，结合红外+微波优于仅微波，生成的频谱更贴近真值，CRPS优于监督式，集合均值与确定性模型相当。

Method: 提出可处理多地球观测源的生成式模型：支持样本间数据源变化、非规则时间间隔、地理错位与不同仪器特性。通过自监督训练：随机遮盖一个来源并重建，实现跨源学习与不确定性建模；并探索仅微波与微波+红外联合训练/推断。评估采用CRPS、功率谱等统计指标，并与监督式和确定性模型比较。

Conclusion: 该工作实现了首个可在不规则时间间隔下融合多微波与红外观测来插值气旋微波影像的生成式方法。相较监督与确定性基线，在不确定性量化与空间统计一致性上更优，推动了热带气旋时空插值与多源遥感融合的发展。

Abstract: Microwave satellite imagery plays a crucial role in monitoring tropical cyclone precipitation and intensity worldwide, but suffers from long revisit times, potentially missing rapid storm evolution phases. While this raises the need for an interpolation method, it is made challenging by the high level of heterogeneity of microwave data coming from different instruments. In this work, we introduce the first generative model that can be applied to multiple geospatial sources that change across samples, occur at irregular time intervals, are misaligned geographically, and come from instruments with varying characteristics. We apply this model to the case of spatio-temporal interpolation of tropical cyclone microwave images from other microwave and infrared instruments. We train using a self-supervised task in which a random source is masked and reconstructed, and show that it leads to a significant decrease in Continuous Ranked Probability Score over supervised training. We show a further improvement by combining infrared and microwave data compared to microwave only. Using these improvements, the generative model produces an ensemble mean on par with that of a deterministic model, while generating a power spectrum significantly closer to that of true observations. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first generative model that interpolates microwave images of cyclones by combining multiple microwave instruments and infrared observations at irregular time intervals.

### [52] [UniRED: Unified RGB-D Video Frame Interpolation with Event Guidance](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24282)
*Yinuo Zhang,Guangshun Wei,Yuanfeng Zhou,Yiran Shen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一个融合RGB、深度与事件数据的统一框架，实现高帧率RGB-D视频插帧，并构建RGB-D-Event数据集；在公开基准与自建数据集上取得更佳的RGB画质与深度几何精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际RGB-D相机受硬件与感测限制，帧率偏低，难以捕捉快速动态；现有仅针对RGB的视频插帧方法直接用于RGB-D会产生边界模糊、伪影与几何一致性差的问题；仅依赖两端帧进行运动估计在复杂动态场景下欠约束。事件相机具有超高时间分辨率，能提供密集运动线索，因而适合弥补上述不足。

Method: 设计统一多模态插帧框架：1) 从RGB、深度和事件数据中提取并融合外观、几何与时间线索；2) 估计双向光流，并进行运动基元（motion basis）细化以提升RGB运动表征，同时对深度进行Z轴向细化以强化几何一致性；3) 通过双向反向映射（warping）和软融合合成目标RGB-D帧。另构建包含三模态的RGB-D-Event数据集用于训练与评测。

Result: 在公开基准和新建数据集上，相比现有方法，RGB插帧获得更高的光度保真度（更清晰、伪影更少），深度插帧获得更强的几何精度（边界更锐利、一致性更好）。

Conclusion: 融合事件相机的时间线索与RGB-D的外观/几何信息，可有效解决低帧率RGB-D插帧中的运动欠约束与几何失真问题；所提框架与数据集共同推动RGB-D视频高帧率重建的性能上限。

Abstract: High frame-rate RGB-D videos are crucial for a variety of downstream tasks, including motion analysis, dynamic scene understanding, and 3D reconstruction. However, due to hardware and sensing constraints, practical RGB-D cameras are typically limited to low frame rates, making it difficult to capture rapid scene dynamics. Existing video interpolation methods have achieved strong performance on RGB data, but they are not readily applicable to RGB-D scenarios, where they often yield blurry boundaries, visible artifacts, and degraded geometric consistency. Furthermore, motion estimation from only two boundary frames is inherently under-constrained in complex dynamic scenes. Event cameras, by contrast, provide asynchronous measurements with ultra-high temporal resolution, offering dense motion cues. In this paper, we propose a unified multimodal framework for RGB-D video interpolation that jointly exploits RGB appearance, depth geometry, and event-based temporal cues. Specifically, it first extracts and fuses RGB, depth and event cues, then estimates bidirectional flow with motion basis refinement for RGB and Z-axial refinement for depth, and finally synthesizes the target RGB-D frame via bidirectional warping and soft blending. In addition, we construct a new RGB-D-Event dataset to alleviate the scarcity of tri-modal training data. Extensive experiments on a public benchmark and the proposed dataset demonstrate that our method achieves superior photometric fidelity for RGB interpolation and stronger geometric accuracy for depth interpolation than existing approaches.

### [53] [ActiveScope: Actively Seeking and Correcting Perception for MLLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24292)
*Yajing Wang,Chao Bi,Junshu Sun,Shufan Shen,Zhaobo Qi,Shuhui Wang,Qingming Huang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出ActiveScope，一个训练免微调的框架，针对高分辨率图像中MLLM细粒度定位困难，通过主动搜索与自校正提升多目标定位与抗干扰能力，显著优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MLLM在高分辨率图像的细粒度感知上易被显著干扰物误导，且在多目标场景下受全局语义偏置影响，难以完整定位多个目标。需要一种无需再训练、能抑制上下文主导与语义偏置的机制。

Method: 提出ActiveScope，包括两大模块：1）Semantic Anchor Localization (SAL)：基于细粒度语义锚独立定位关键目标，降低语义偏置；2）Interference-Suppressed Refinement (ISR)：在细化阶段抑制对显著干扰物的注意力，克服上下文主导。整体为训练免、主动搜索与自我纠错范式。

Result: 在多项高分辨率图像理解基准上优于现有训练免方法，例如在V* Bench上达到96.34%准确率，展现更强的多目标与抗干扰定位能力。

Conclusion: 通过主动搜索与自校正并结合语义锚定位与干扰抑制细化，ActiveScope有效缓解语义偏置和上下文主导问题，显著提升MLLM在高分辨率视觉-语言任务中的细粒度感知与多目标定位性能。

Abstract: Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have demonstrated impressive vision-language understanding, yet still struggle with fine-grained perception in high-resolution images. While existing training-free methods typically rely on attention-based localization or coarse-to-fine search, they are often misled by distractors and fail to locate multiple targets. Our investigation attributes these failures to Contextual Dominance, where salient distractors overwhelm target attention and cause inaccurate localization, and Semantic Bias, where global semantics cause the model to fixate on the most salient concept, resulting in incomplete localization in multi-object scenarios. Built on these insights, we propose ActiveScope, a training-free framework that enhances MLLMs by actively seeking and correcting perception. ActiveScope features two modules. The Semantic Anchor Localization (SAL) utilizes fine-grained semantic anchors to independently localize key targets, thereby mitigating semantic bias. The Interference-Suppressed Refinement (ISR) refines localization by suppressing attention on salient distractions to overcome contextual dominance. Extensive experiments on high-resolution image understanding benchmarks demonstrate that ActiveScope outperforms existing training-free methods (e.g., 96.34 percent accuracy on $V^{*}$ Bench), validating the superiority of the active search and self-correction paradigm. Our code is available at https://github.com/jasmine-ww/ActiveScope.

</details>


### [54] [Hierarchical Spatial and Channel Aggregation for Cross-domain Few-shot Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24296)
*Sujun Sun,Mingwu Ren,Haofeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出DHANet用于跨域小样本分割，通过空间与通道双层级聚合缓解语义/属性过对齐，并引入在线概率语义库从查询中构造伪原型增强支撑信息，在多数据集上取得SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CD-FSS方法多仅处理风格/分布偏移，忽视不同域之间类别语义粒度与判别属性差异，导致支持-查询匹配出现语义过对齐（细粒度语义被抹平）与属性过对齐（判别属性被误对齐），从而削弱泛化与精度。

Method: 提出Dual Hierarchical Aggregation Network (DHANet)：1) HSA模块：在空间维度进行多尺度区域/层级聚合，生成语义增强的层级特征以缓解语义过对齐；2) HCA模块：在通道维度进行多尺度属性聚合，形成属性增强的层级特征以缓解属性过对齐；3) 在线概率语义库OPSB：在推理阶段从查询预测动态统计类别概率分布，构建并更新伪原型，作为额外支撑信息以弥补支撑不足。整体提升跨域支持-查询匹配的鲁棒性。

Result: 在四个目标域数据集上进行广泛实验，方法在CD-FSS任务上取得了最新最优（SOTA）性能，相比以往方法显著提升分割精度。

Conclusion: 通过空间与通道的双层级聚合有效解决跨域语义与属性过对齐问题，结合在线概率语义库缓解支撑稀缺，整体显著提升跨域小样本分割的泛化与准确性。

Abstract: Cross-domain Few-shot Segmentation (CD-FSS) aims to learn generalizable segmentation capability from abundant annotated samples in the source domain, enabling accurate segmentation of novel classes in the target domain with only a few annotated samples. Existing CD-FSS methods mainly focus on mitigating feature distribution shifts caused by style gaps while ignoring significant differences in class semantic granularity and discriminative attributes across domains, leading to two key degradations in support-query matching: semantic over-alignment and attribute over-alignment. To this end, we propose the Dual Hierarchical Aggregation Network (DHANet), which comprises three key modules. First, the Hierarchical Spatial Aggregation (HSA) module performs multi-scale region aggregation of pixel features along the spatial dimension, generating hierarchical semantic-enhanced features to alleviate semantic over-alignment. Additionally, the HCA module conducts multi-scale attribute aggregation along the channel dimension, generating hierarchical attribute-enhanced features to mitigate attribute over-alignment. Finally, we propose the Online Probabilistic Semantic Bank (OPSB), which progressively constructs and updates class probability distributions from query predictions during inference, and samples multiple pseudo-prototypes as additional support information to mitigate insufficient support. Extensive experiments on four target-domain datasets demonstrate that our method achieves state-of-the-art performance.

### [55] [Training-free Cross-domain Few-shot Segmentation via Robust Semantic Representation and Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24297)
*Sujun Sun,Mingwu Ren,Haofeng Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一个基于DINOv3的零训练（training-free）跨域小样本分割框架，通过三模块提升跨域泛化：SAFR进行语义重融、ASE利用查询增强支持、HPM混合原型匹配；在四个目标域上达到SOTA表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CD-FSS方法需训练或微调，计算开销大且易过拟合；引入大视觉基础模型后仍可能过拟合、收益有限。需要一种无需训练、能有效跨域泛化的方案。

Method: 以自监督视觉编码器DINOv3为 backbone，设计三大无训练模块：1) SAFR：从多层/多尺度特征中识别强调语义模式的通道或空间成分并重融，提升语义可判别性；2) ASE：从查询图像聚合稳健语义信息来自适应增强支持特征，缩小支持-查询语义鸿沟；3) HPM：构造多种原型（如全局/局部、单/多峰），融合其匹配结果以适应不同域的语义复杂度。整体流水线仅做前向推理与度量匹配，无可学习参数。

Result: 在四个不同目标域数据集上进行广泛实验，方法在无任何训练的条件下取得了SOTA的CD-FSS性能，优于需训练/微调的现有方法。

Conclusion: 通过去参数化与三模块设计（SAFR、ASE、HPM），可在无需训练的条件下有效解决跨域小样本分割的过拟合与计算开销问题，并在多域上实现强泛化与SOTA表现。

Abstract: Cross-domain Few-shot Segmentation (CD-FSS) aims to transfer knowledge learned from source domain to distinct target domains, segmenting unseen target classes with only a few annotated samples. Although existing methods have made significant progress, they still rely on training or fine-tuning processes, which incur high computational costs and risk overfitting. We observe that when powerful and general-purpose vision foundation models are incorporated into these methods, their performance shows only marginal improvement or even degrades due to overfitting. To address this, we eliminate trainable parameters and propose a training-free framework to avoid both training overhead and overfitting. Built upon the self-supervised vision encoder DINOv3, our framework addresses cross-domain challenges through three core modules. First, the Semantic-aware Feature Re-fusion (SAFR) module identifies and re-fuses features that emphasize semantic patterns, generating representations with enhanced semantic discriminability. Additionally, the Adaptive Support Enhancement (ASE) module narrows semantic gaps between support and query through robust query information aggregation. Finally, the Hybrid Prototype Matching (HPM) module integrates matching results from diverse prototypes to adapt to varying semantic complexity across domains. Extensive experiments on four target domain datasets demonstrate that our method achieves state-of-the-art performance in CD-FSS without any training.

### [56] [MM-TRELLIS: Point-Cloud Guided Multi-Modal 3D Vehicle Generation in Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24301)
*Hongli Xiao,Youjian Zhang,Yucai Bai,Chaoyue Wang,Yaohui Jin,Xiaoguang Ren,Wenjing Yang,Long Lan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MM-TRELLIS：利用多视角图像与LiDAR引导的原生3D生成方法，面向真实自动驾驶场景的高保真车辆模型重建；通过点云对齐与一致性约束及基于3D高斯不透明度的体素滤波，生成干净网格，性能优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于TRELLIS扩展为多模态：1) 将多视角图像循环作为条件输入；2) 在去噪过程引入LiDAR点云的测试时引导：先将点云与模型先验对齐，再对生成几何施加与点云的一致性约束；3) 使用基于3D Gaussian Splatting不透明度的体素滤波，抑制浮点噪声（floaters），输出干净网格。

Result: 在Waymo数据集上进行全面实验，MM-TRELLIS在高保真3D车辆生成方面优于现有方法（更好的几何准确性、跨视一致性与网格干净度）。代码已开源。

Abstract: Recovering realistic 3D vehicle models from autonomous driving scenes is crucial for synthesizing training data and building simulation environment. However, most existing vehicle generation methods fail to fully exploit multimodal sensors i.e. multi-view images and LiDAR point clouds) and rely on neural rendering based reconstruction, leading to low-quality mesh. Recently, native 3D generative models have made significant progress, yet they are not built for arbitrary multi-view inputs and often struggle with in-the-wild driving images. In this work, we present MM-TRELLIS, a multi-modal version of TRELLIS for in-the-wild 3D vehicle generation that integrates LiDAR and image sensors from autonomous driving datasets into native 3D generative models. Specifically, multi-view images are cycled as conditioning inputs, while LiDAR point clouds provide test-time guidance to ensure geometric accuracy and cross-view consistency. During denoising, we first align the guidance point cloud with the model priors, then enforce consistency between the generated geometry and the guidance point cloud. Finally, we introduce a voxel filtering strategy based on the opacity of 3D Gaussian Splatting to suppress floaters and produce clean meshes. Comprehensive experiments on Waymo dataset demonstrate our method outperforms existing methods in high-fidelity 3D vehicle generation. Code is available at https://github.com/HongliXiao/MM-TRELLIS.

### [57] [TrOCR for Medieval HTR: A Systematic Ablation Study with Cross-Dataset Validation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24302)
*Sachin Sharma,Michele Flammini,Federico Simonetta*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 研究在小型中世纪手稿数据上微调TrOCR时，三种可控策略（对比度归一化、数据增强、层冻结）对识别精度的影响；最佳配置在Cortonese上达8.03% CER，去掉CLAHE达7.84% CER；浅层冻结无显著伤害，深度冻结有害；解码器冻结的可迁移性优于编码器；用Grad-CAM与交叉注意力分析错误模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer式HTR模型多在现代文本上预训练，迁移到中世纪手稿这类视觉域差异巨大的任务时适配困难。实际研究者面对小样本历史数据集，常依赖图像预处理、数据增强或冻结层数，但缺少系统性的量化比较和可迁移性评估。本文旨在给出可操作的微调策略证据与诊断工具。

Method: 以TrOCR为基底，围绕三类可控选择构建13种配置：是否使用对比度限制自适应直方图均衡化（CLAHE）、不同强度的数据增强、以及分别对编码器与解码器冻结不同深度的层数。主要在13世纪意大利手稿I-CT 91（“Cortonese”）上进行受控实验，并在READ-16基准上复现实验网格以检验鲁棒性。通过统计比较（显著性检验）评估各配置差异，并利用Grad-CAM与解码器交叉注意力可视化分析错误与失效模式。

Result: 在Cortonese上最佳常规微调配置达8.03% CER；去除CLAHE后可达7.84% CER，与领域专用基线相当，表明强优化可减少对图像预处理的依赖。冻结至多3层编码器或6层解码器对精度无显著影响，进一步加深冻结会逐步恶化表现。跨数据集验证显示：解码器冻结阈值的可迁移性优于编码器，且编码器与解码器的组合冻结需要针对数据集重新验证。

Conclusion: 在小型历史手稿HTR的TrOCR迁移中，浅层冻结是安全的，深度冻结有风险；强优化可替代部分预处理（如CLAHE）；解码器冻结策略更具跨数据集稳健性。建议在新数据集上优先微调解码器或进行轻度冻结，并用梯度与注意力可视化来定位错误模式。源码已开源。

Abstract: Fine-tuning transformer-based handwritten text recognition (HTR) models on medieval manuscripts is challenging because these models are pre-trained on modern text and must adapt to a very different visual domain. This paper studies how three controllable fine-tuning choices (contrast normalization, data augmentation, and layer freezing) affect recognition accuracy when adapting TrOCR to small historical datasets. We run controlled experiments on a 13th-century Italian manuscript (I-CT 91 "Cortonese") and replicate the same experimental grid on the public READ-16 benchmark as robustness evidence. On Cortonese, our best configuration achieves 8.03% character error rate (CER). Statistical comparisons across 13 configurations show that freezing up to three encoder layers or six decoder layers does not significantly harm accuracy, while deeper freezing becomes progressively detrimental. Removing contrast normalization (CLAHE) yields 7.84% CER, comparable to a domain-specialized baseline, suggesting strong optimization can reduce reliance on image preprocessing. Cross-dataset validation on READ-16 shows that decoder freezing thresholds transfer more robustly than encoder thresholds, and combined freezing strategies require dataset-specific re-validation. Finally, we use Grad-CAM gradient attributions and decoder cross-attention maps to diagnose error patterns and failure modes revealed by the ablations. Source code is available at https://github.com/LaudareProject/TrOCR-analysis

### [58] [REDI-Match: Rotation-Equivariant Distillation for Efficient and Robust Dense Matching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24330)
*Yinji Ge,Guixu Zheng,Wulong Guo,Qian Feng,Xu Wu,Kai Zhou,Xinyuan Liu,Fei Xing*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出REDI-Match：用旋转等变蒸馏将VFM语义迁移到轻量等变编码器，并在解码端用熵驱动的离散旋转假设锁定坐标，显著提升强旋转场景匹配精度与速度，达SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 密集特征匹配在强平面内旋转下表现不佳。数据驱动方法需大规模参数/数据去“学”旋转，效率低；严格等变网络又缺乏现代VFM的高层语义。主流做法冻结VFM，将旋转泛化压力完全推给解码器，形成架构瓶颈，需新方法兼顾等变性与语义表达。

Method: 提出旋转等变蒸馏（REDI）：将非等变VFM的高语义表示蒸馏到轻量、严格旋转等变的编码器（基于等变几何架构约束高维语义）；为解码器加入熵驱动的空间对齐模块，通过评估离散旋转假设显式锁定标准坐标系，随后进行连续细化，消除全局旋转歧义。

Result: 在多项基准上达成SOTA；在SatAst数据集上绝对位姿精度提升13.89%，且较RoMa v2推理快1.9倍，在单张RTX 4090上可实时约41 FPS。

Conclusion: 通过将VFM语义与严格旋转等变性解耦并以蒸馏重组，再辅以熵驱动的显式旋转假设搜索，REDI-Match打破现有架构瓶颈，在强旋转场景显著提升精度与效率，具备实用实时性。

Abstract: Vision Foundation Models (VFMs) have significantly advanced dense feature matching, yet severe in-plane rotation remains a critical challenge. Existing solutions face a fundamental dilemma: data-driven methods require inefficient parameter scaling to implicitly learn rotations, whereas strictly equivariant networks lack the semantic capacity of modern VFMs. Consequently, current frameworks typically freeze VFMs and shift the entire burden of rotation generalization to the downstream decoder. To break this architectural bottleneck, we propose REDI-Match, an efficient framework driven by a novel Rotation-Equivariant Distillation (REDI) paradigm. Instead of relying on rotation data augmentation to establish rotational correspondences, REDI distills the non-equivariant semantic representations of a VFM into a lightweight, strictly rotation-equivariant encoder, leveraging an equivariant geometric architecture to constrain robust high-dimensional semantics. To fully exploit these features, we equip the decoder with an entropy-driven spatial alignment module. By evaluating discrete rotation hypotheses, this mechanism explicitly locks onto the canonical coordinate system, eliminating global ambiguity before continuous refinement. Extensive experiments demonstrate that REDI-Match establishes a new state-of-the-art (SOTA) across multiple benchmarks. Notably, it achieves a 13.89% absolute pose accuracy improvement on the highly challenging SatAst dataset while operating 1.9x faster than the current SOTA (RoMa v2), enabling real-time inference (~41 FPS) on a single RTX 4090 GPU. Code: https://github.com/YinjiGe/REDI-Match.

### [59] [UniTranslator: A Unified Multi-modal Framework for End-to-end In-Image Machine Translation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24333)
*Jiahao Lyu,Pei Fu,Zhenhang Li,Shaojie Zhang,Jiahui Yang,Yu Zhou,Can Ma,Zhenbo Luo,Jian Luan*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 统一多模态模型虽可同时理解与生成，但直接用于IIMT会出现两大痛点：1) 理解-生成冲突（翻译语义与生成监督不一致）；2) 空间位置失配（渲染文字与目标区域不对齐）。需要一个能在语义与空间上同时对齐的端到端方案。

Method: 提出UniTranslator包含两大关键组件：1) UGAM（Understand-Generation Alignment Module），在表示层面对齐理解与生成，促使翻译预测与渲染文本语义一致；2) SMD（Spatial Mask Decoder），提供像素级文本区域监督，提升空间落点、几何对齐与版式可控性。框架在统一多模态模型上耦合翻译理解与文本编辑训练。

Result: 在多个基准、跨多语向与复杂真实版面上取得SOTA。实验显示理解与生成之间存在显著的相互增强效应。

Conclusion: 通过语义对齐（UGAM）与空间对齐（SMD），统一训练可同时提升翻译正确性与图像渲染质量，验证了统一翻译-生成学习在IIMT任务中的优势。

Abstract: In-Image Machine Translation (IIMT) aims to translate scene text in an image and render the translated text back into the original regions while preserving the overall visual appearance. Recent unified multimodal models provide a promising solution by combining visual-text understanding and image generation within a single framework. However, directly adapting such models to IIMT remains challenging. In particular, they often suffer from understanding-generation conflicts, where the translation inferred during understanding is inconsistent with the text supervision used in generation, and spatial position misalignment, where the rendered text does not accurately match the target text regions. To address these issues, we present UniTranslator, a unified multimodal framework for IIMT that tightly couples translation understanding and text editing. Specifically, we introduce an Understand-Generation Alignment Module (UGAM) to bridge the representation gap between understanding and generation, encouraging semantic consistency between translated content prediction and text rendering. We further propose a Spatial Mask Decoder (SMD) with pixel-level supervision over text regions to improve spatial grounding, geometric alignment, and layout controllability during generation. Extensive experiments on multiple benchmarks demonstrate that UniTranslator achieves state-of-the-art performance across diverse language directions and complex real-world layouts. Moreover, our results reveal a strong mutual reinforcement effect between translation understanding and image generation, highlighting the advantage of unified translation multimodal learning. Code is available at https://github.com/SeerRay-Lab/Unitranslator.

### [60] [Ill-Posed by Design: Probing Evidence Use in VLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24335)
*Boaz Meivar,Shaked Perek,Shani Shvartzman,Eli Schwartz,Shai Avidan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出将“单目度量物体尺寸估计”作为诊断VLM证据选择的病态任务，并构建Metric VQA数据集与反事实分解实验，发现即便最大VLM也落后于文本LLM；最关键线索是目标身份，像素与局部上下文只对部分模型有益，表观尺寸会影响但无方向性，场景几何基本未被利用；LoRA可学到任务但仍未学会利用几何。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统反事实分析在良定任务上诊断力有限：多条独立线索可支撑同一答案，移除一条预测可能不变。作者转而选择病态设定：单目、未校准图像无法唯一确定物理尺寸，模型被迫依赖不完美证据（类先验、目标外观、局部上下文、表观尺寸、场景几何等），更能检验模型如何选证与用证。

Method: 1) 定义单目度量尺寸问答任务；2) 构建Metric VQA数据集：来自Objectron的10,813个“维度”查询与331个实测（卷尺测量）野外场景；3) 评测12个开源大规模VLM（3–397B）；4) 设计反事实分解，隔离六类证据通道（语言/目标身份、目标像素、局部上下文、表观图像尺寸、全局场景几何等），观察移除/操控对预测的影响；5) 尝试针对性LoRA微调以提升度量估计能力。

Result: - 在野外分割上，即便最大VLM（Qwen3-VL-235B、Qwen3.5-397B、InternVL3.5-241B）也落后于仅文本前沿LLM；- 证据负载排序：目标身份最关键；目标像素与局部上下文仅对部分模型有效；表观尺寸能改变预测但缺乏一致方向读出；全局场景几何基本未被使用；- LoRA微调能学到任务本身，但并未促使模型有效利用几何信息。

Conclusion: 单目度量尺寸估计为诊断VLM证据选择的有效病态基准。当前VLM主要依赖语义先验而非几何推理，限制了在现实场景中的度量能力。即使通过LoRA可提升表现，模型仍未学会系统性利用场景几何，提示未来需引入几何感知表示、标定/深度辅助或专门训练目标以提升度量与可解释性。

Abstract: Counterfactual analysis is widely used to study evidence use in vision-language models, but its diagnostic value is limited on well-posed tasks: when several cues independently support the same answer, removing one may not change the prediction. We propose monocular metric object-size estimation as an ill-posed diagnostic setting for evidence selection: because physical size cannot be determined from a single uncalibrated image, models must rely on imperfect cues category priors, target appearance, local context, apparent image size, and scene geometry. We assemble Metric VQA ($10{,}813$ dimension queries from Objectron and $331$ tape-measured in-the-wild scenes) and evaluate $12$ open-weight VLMs ($3$--$397$\,B parameters) with counterfactual analysis decomposing six visual and language evidence channels. Even the largest VLMs tested (Qwen3-VL-235B, Qwen3.5-397B, InternVL3.5-241B) trail a text-only frontier LLM on the in-the-wild split. The diagnostic analysis shows: target identity is the most load-bearing cue, target pixels and local context help only some models, apparent size shifts predictions without a directional readout, and global scene geometry is largely unused. We analyze LoRA fine-tuning as an actionable intervention specific to metric estimation: while the task is learnable, the models do not learn to leverage scene geometry.

</details>


### [61] [TIGER: Taming Identity, Geometry, and Generative Priors for High-Quality Face Video Restoration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24336)
*Yang Zhou,Wenxue Li,Peng Zhang,Yifei Chen,Fei Wang,Daiguo Zhou*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: TIGER是一个融合身份、几何与生成三重先验的面部视频修复框架，通过身份锚定、三维几何解耦与一步整流生成先验，并配合三阶段训练，在身份一致性、时序稳定与感知质量上达到SOTA。

Method: 提出TIGER三先验融合：1) 身份先验：将区分性身份嵌入注入潜空间，在强退化下锚定主体身份；2) 几何先验：把2D参考线索升维到解耦的3D参数空间，并通过跨源参数融合形成稳定几何锚点，实现时序一致的结构引导；3) 生成先验：利用视频生成模型的一步rectified flow以高效方式提升写实度。并设计三阶段渐进式训练，依次优化结构保真、纹理重建与分布级真实感；同时构建大规模FVR数据集用于训练与评测。

Result: 在广泛实验中，TIGER在身份保真度与时间稳定性上取得SOTA，并兼具高质量与高效率；项目页提供定性与定量结果。

Conclusion: 通过结构化三先验融合与渐进训练，TIGER有效缓解身份漂移与视角耦合问题，在保持身份一致的同时提升时序与感知质量，为高效高质量的面部视频修复提供新范式。

Abstract: Face Video Restoration (FVR) aims to recover high-fidelity facial videos from degraded input while preserving identity and semantic consistency across frames. Existing methods often struggle to simultaneously address three key challenges: identity shift, viewpoint-entangled guidance, and perceptual realism. To tackle these issues, we propose TIGER, a structured tri-prior fusion framework that Tames Identity, Geometry, and gEnerative pRiors for high-quality FVR. Specifically, an Identity Prior is first established by injecting subject-discriminative embeddings into the latent space, effectively anchoring the subject's identity against severe degradations. Then, to provide temporally consistent structural guidance for dynamic videos, TIGER constructs a Geometry Prior by lifting 2D reference cues into a disentangled 3D parameter space, creating a geometric anchor through cross-source parameter fusion. Moreover, to achieve maximum efficiency without compromising realism, we harness the video generation model's Generative Prior through a one-step rectified flow. We further design a progressive three-stage training optimization strategy that refines structural fidelity, textural reconstruction, and distribution-level realism to ensure robust optimization. We also construct a large-scale FVR dataset to facilitate robust training and standardized evaluation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that TIGER achieves state-of-the-art performance in both identity fidelity and temporal stability, delivering a high-quality, efficient and identity-consistent FVR. Project page: https://yzhoulv.github.io/Tiger/.

### [62] [Open-Vocabulary BEV Segmentation with 3D-Aware Geometric Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24353)

  <summary>Details</summary>

A key challenge in OVBS lies in the 3D geometric inconsistency inherent in the ill-posed lifting of 2D VLM semantics into BEV. To address this, we propose OVBEVSeg, a geometry-aware OVBS framework that enhances efficient Gaussian splatting (GS)-based unprojection by leveraging robust 3D geometric constraints across three progressive stages: (1) 2D-to-BEV pseudo-labeling via reliable 3D projection for OV generalization; (2) joint 2D-BEV per-scene optimization with BEV structural constraints for 3D geometric consistency; and (3) 3D geometric distillation for online efficiency. Furthermore, it achieves 2.5x faster inference with only 0.22x the memory consumption of projection-based methods. Project page: https://hchoi256.github.io/projects/ovbevseg/.

Conclusion: 大规模、三轴向的合成与后处理增强能显著提升手语模型对真实世界分布偏移的鲁棒性。SignNet-1M连同完整增强流水线与统一基准为社区提供可复现、可扩展的训练与评测资源，助力更强的跨域泛化。

Abstract: Sign language models are typically trained on datasets captured under constrained conditions, with limited viewpoint, background, and signer-identity diversity, leading to poor robustness under real-world distribution shifts. We introduce SignNet-1M, a large-scale augmented dataset spanning ASL, CSL, and German Sign Language (DGS). SignNet-1M synthesizes realistic variations along three axes: (i) novel-view rendering (rotation and zoom) via 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS), (ii) scene/identity editing via diffusion models for background replacement and signer substitution while preserving sign motion and linguistic content, and (iii) post-rendering augmentations that emulate capture and compression artifacts (e.g., pose/temporal perturbations and video-level corruptions) to better match in-the-wild recordings. Beyond data release, we provide a unified benchmark suite across downstream tasks (e.g., translation and recognition) and ablations that isolate each augmentation component. ### [64] [Structural Kolmogorov-Arnold Convolutions: Learnable Function on the Values or the Filter Shape as Parameter-Efficient Alternative to Per-Edge Convolutional KANs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24371)
*Stefano Mereu,Oleksandr Kuznetsov,Gabriele Marchello,Alessandro Galdelli,Emanuele Frontoni,Adriano Mancini,Ferdinando Cannella*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出将卷积核中“可学习函数”的位置从逐像素数值边上，转移到卷积的结构（尤其是滤波器形状）上；在相同小规模设置下，形状驱动的RF-KAN与最简单的数值共享SV-KAN效果最佳，且优于多种逐边KAN与普通卷积，同时更省参数。关键增益来自局部振荡基与内容自适应；去除可学习形状会导致准确率大幅崩塌。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有KAN式卷积常为每个核权重配一个一元函数，表达力强但参数巨多、易过拟合。作者认为应把可学习性注入卷积的结构（滤波器形状）而非逐边权重，并系统化比较“作用于像素值vs作用于滤波器形状”的两端设计。

Method: 提出并对比三种实现：1) SV-KAN：对像素值施加一个共享一元函数，空间滤波器固定不变，相当于共享激活函数的普通卷积；2) AG-KAN：仍用共享值函数，但通过内容自适应高斯门提供空间结构；3) RF-KAN：把可学习函数移到滤波器形状，用定向脊线轮廓，并在局部化的振荡（Morlet小波）基上展开，幅度做内容自适应。统一四层协议、三种随机种子、内置参考对照，控制参数规模约0.4M。

Result: 在CIFAR-10上：RF-KAN 88.47±0.10%，SV-KAN 88.20±0.31%；在CIFAR-100上：RF-KAN 64.40±0.19%，SV-KAN 64.57±0.30%；两者均优于普通卷积和多种逐边KAN（含官方Gram变体），且参数仅其约五分之一。剖析表明RF-KAN的优势来自局部化振荡基与内容自适应。去除可学习形状、仅留共享值函数时，准确率下降逾40个百分点，说明形状学习在该规模下是核心负载。

Conclusion: 将可学习性放到滤波器形状上是有效的设计轴。RF-KAN与最简SV-KAN在小模型下达到最佳且更省参，优于逐边KAN。RF-KAN的收益来源被定位为局部振荡基+内容自适应；学习到的形状是关键因素。

Abstract: Convolutional Kolmogorov--Arnold Networks (KANs) replace the fixed weights of a convolutional kernel with learnable univariate functions. The dominant formulation attaches one such function to every kernel entry and lets it act on pixel values, expressive but parameter-heavy and prone to overfitting. We argue that the learnable functions are better placed in the \emph{structure} of the convolution than on each edge, and we organise the design space along a single axis: whether the function acts on the pixel \emph{values} or on the filter \emph{shape}. We study three realisations. SV-KAN applies one shared univariate function to the values and leaves the spatial filter free and static, aa classical convolution with a single learnable shared activation. AG-KAN keeps the shared value function but supplies the spatial structure through a content-adaptive Gaussian gate. RF-KAN instead moves the learnable functions onto the filter shape, building each filter from oriented ridge profiles expanded in a localised oscillatory (Morlet) wavelet basis with content-adaptive amplitudes. Under a matched four-layer protocol with in-run references and three seeds, RF-KAN and SV-KAN reach $88.47\pm0.10\%$ and $88.20\pm0.31\%$ on CIFAR-10 and $64.40\pm0.19\%$ and $64.57\pm0.30\%$ on CIFAR-100, at about $0.4$M parameters. At this matched scale the shape model and the simplest value model meet at the top, both above a plain convolution and every per-edge KAN we tested, including the official Gram variant, at roughly a fifth of the parameters. A controlled study attributes the RF-KAN gain to an intrinsically localised oscillatory basis and to content adaptivity, and an ablation that removes the learned shape entirely, leaving only the shared value function, collapses accuracy by over forty points, identifying the learned shape as the load-bearing ingredient at this scale.

</details>


### [65] [MATCH: Flow Matching for Multi-View Anomaly Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24375)
*Mathis Kruse,Melissa Schween,Bodo Rosenhahn*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出MATCH：首个基于Flow Matching（FM）的多视角工业异常检测方法，可在对象、图像与像素级利用ODE形式估计似然并给出异常分数；在Real-IAD与MANTA-Tiny上达SOTA，且可在消费级硬件与实时场景运行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工业场景中复杂物体需多视角检测异常，现有方法在效率、精度与可解释层级（对象/图像/像素）方面受限；需要一种既能多尺度处理、又能提供基于概率的统一异常评分、并能在实际生产中高效运行的方法。

Method: 以Flow Matching的常微分方程（ODE）表述为核心：将多视角图像提取的多尺度特征通过FM映射到高斯分布，利用可估计的似然构造对象、图像与像素级异常分数。利用FM的架构灵活性处理不同空间分辨率特征；为满足实时性，舍弃用于精确似然的散度项，提出近似但高效的评分。并进行多项消融验证设计选择。

Result: 在Real-IAD进行系统评测并取得SOTA的检测与分割表现；首次在MANTA-Tiny上做全面评估并同样获得领先结果；在消费级硬件上可实时运行。

Conclusion: 基于FM的MATCH在多视角异常检测中实现统一的似然驱动评分、跨尺度特征对齐与高效推理，达成SOTA性能与实用性；消融研究支持其关键设计。

Abstract: Detecting anomalies in industrial objects is an important topic for increasing production efficiency. More complex objects often require the analysis of several view points, which has led to the field of multi-view anomaly detection. We present MATCH, the first multi-view anomaly detection method based on Flow Matching (FM). With the ODE formulation of Flow Matching, we can estimate likelihoods and thereby derive an anomaly score to detect anomalies in multi-view image data at object, image, and pixel-level. The architectural flexibility of FM models allows us to efficiently transform features of different spatial sizes to the normal distribution. We evaluate thoroughly on the already established Real-IAD data set and are also the first to provide a comprehensive evaluation of popular anomaly detection methods for the MANTA-Tiny data set. MATCH achieves state-of-the-art performance in both anomaly detection and segmentation, all while running on consumer-level hardware. By omitting the costly divergence term needed for likelihood estimation, we ensure that MATCH is usable in real-time production scenarios. Lastly, several ablation studies are conducted to validate the methodological choices.

### [66] [Modality-Aware Out-of-Distribution Detection for Multi-Modal Action Recognition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24404)
*Lars Doorenbos,Duc Manh Vu,Serdar Ozsoy,Juergen Gall*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种专为多模态场景设计的后验（post-hoc）OOD检测器，将多模态与单模态预测关系的信号与多模态特征空间的离流形分数融合，并用多模态logits归一化，兼容现有训练期方法，在MultiOOD等基准上平均超越SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态能提升动作识别性能，但其对鲁棒性、特别是多模态OOD检测的作用研究不足。现有方法即便在训练时考虑OOD，推理仍使用单模态OOD检测器，忽视多模态间的信息关系，导致性能受限。

Method: 1) 发现并利用多模态与单模态预测之间的特定关系，构造一种面向多模态的后验检测信号；2) 计算多模态特征空间中的离流形（off-manifold）分数；3) 将上述信号与分数进行融合，并用多模态logits进行归一化；4) 作为推理阶段的混合检测器，可与任意训练期正则化/方法兼容。

Result: 在MultiOOD基准的多种数据集与设定上，一致提升OOD检测性能，平均优于现有最先进方法，表现稳定。

Conclusion: 推理阶段显式建模与利用不同模态的信息对于多模态OOD检测至关重要；所提混合后验检测器简单、兼容现有训练流程并带来持续的SOTA水平提升。

Abstract: The incorporation of additional modalities into action recognition models increases their performance across a wide range of settings. However, how this additional information can contribute to making the models more robust remains underexplored, particularly for the case of multi-modal out-of-distribution (OOD) detection. While methods exist that regularize the multi-modal training process with OOD detection in mind, they still apply off-the-shelf OOD detectors designed for the uni-modal case during inference, discarding important information. Based on an interesting relationship we find between the multi-modal and uni-modal predictions, we propose to use this signal to build a post-hoc detector explicitly designed for the multi-modal scenario. We combine this new source of information with a feature-space score, which detects off-manifold samples in the multi-modal space, and normalize them by the multi-modal logits. In doing so, the proposed hybrid detector is compatible with existing training-time approaches and consistently improves performance. Experiments on a wide range of established datasets from the MultiOOD benchmark show that, on average, our approach outperforms the state of the art. Our results show the importance of explicitly considering the different modalities at inference time for multi-modal OOD detection.

### [67] [EgoSAT: A Comprehensive Benchmark of Egocentric Streaming Interaction Understanding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24422)
*Yijia Lei,Jinzhao Li,Yichi Zhang,Jiacheng Hua,Yin Li,Miao Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: EgoSAT 是首个面向流式自我视角视频推理的综合基准，统一评测模型对过去-现在-未来的理解与预测能力，并揭示当前VLM在可回答性与置信度校准上的显著缺陷。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLM多在离线设定或单一任务上评估，难以反映真实交互中视频帧按时间顺序到达、且需同时进行回顾（已发生）、在线（进行中）与前瞻（将发生）的连续理解需求。缺乏统一框架衡量模型在流式交互理解中的综合推理与校准能力。

Method: 构建EgoSAT基准：在严格的流式约束下（只能访问已观察到的帧），将回顾性、在线性与前瞻性问题统一为一套问答式评测；收集1997段、总计165小时的第一人称视频及约4800条高质量QA，覆盖不同时间上下文；对多种开源与闭源VLM进行系统评测，并区分“可回答性”，结合模型置信度进行诊断与误校准分析。

Result: 在EgoSAT上，现有VLM在前瞻与回顾推理上表现不佳，且普遍存在严重的置信度误校准：模型的置信度与问题的内在可回答性不一致，常出现“自信但错误”的风险行为。

Conclusion: EgoSAT为评估流式自我视角视频推理提供统一而严格的基准，揭示当前VLM在时序综合推理与置信度校准方面的明显短板，为后续改进在线理解、事件记忆与不确定性估计方法指明方向。

Abstract: We introduce EgoSAT, the first comprehensive benchmark for egocentric video reasoning in streaming settings, designed to evaluate the capabilities of modern vision-language models (VLMs). The benchmark targets streaming interaction understanding, where video frames arrive sequentially and models must continuously interpret evolving visual context. EgoSAT unifies several previously distinct tasks within a single streaming framework. In this formulation, queries about completed events correspond to retrospective reasoning, queries about ongoing activities require online understanding, and queries about future actions involve prospective anticipation. This unified setting requires models to reason about the past, present, and future while operating under the constraint that only previously observed frames are available. EgoSAT contains 1,997 unique videos spanning 165 hours of egocentric footage and around 4,800 high-quality question-answer pairs, carefully designed to probe reasoning across varying temporal contexts. Using this benchmark, we evaluate a diverse set of both open-weight and closed-weight VLMs, providing a systematic assessment of their ability for streaming interaction understanding. By distinguishing answerability and conducting diagnostics on confidence of models, we find existing models not only struggle with prospective and retrospective modeling, but also exhibit severe mis-calibration: confidence often fails to track inherent answerability, leading to dangerous "confidently wrong" behaviors. Project page: https://leiyj23.github.io/EgoSAT/

</details>


### [68] [Transformation Behavior of Images in Latent Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24430)
*Christian Zöllner,Mozzam Motiwala,Aysel Ahadova,Gerrit Anders,Robert Hüneburg,Jacob Nattermann,Matthias Kloor*

TL;DR: 研究评估病理图像编码器对经典图像变换的鲁棒性与不变性，发现变换后嵌入与原图更接近而非随机，但仍非完全不变；病理特定编码器与通用编码器表现存在显著差异。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 选用三类预训练编码器（Lunit、Bioptimus 的病理专用与 Meta 的通用），对结直肠组织及 TCGA H&E 切片瓦片进行标准图像变换（如旋转、翻转、缩放、颜色扰动等），比较原始与变换后嵌入的距离，并与随机不相关图像嵌入对比，以量化鲁棒性/不变性差异。

Result: 原图与变换图的嵌入距离显著小于其与随机图的距离，显示对变换具有鲁棒性；但仍存在可测差异，说明未实现完全不变。通用编码器与病理特定编码器在不变性程度与稳定性上存在显著差别（病理特定编码器通常更稳健）。

Conclusion: 现有编码器对常见图像变换具备一定鲁棒性但不完全不变，因而基于变换的数据增强仍能提升下游性能；选择或训练与任务匹配的病理专用编码器更有利，并应在训练中显式鼓励对标签无关变换的不变性。

Abstract: Training of neural networks for histopathology classification tasks typically relies on data encoding into latent space, which reduces complexity and improves performance. There are several encoder networks available, either pretrained on general image datasets such as ImageNET, or specifically on histopathological images. Training of encoder networks should be adapted to downstream tasks, allowing encoding of biologic/diagnostic content while rendering networks invariant to label-irrelevant transformations.
  This paper investigates the effect of classical image transformation on the latent space, using networks provided by Lunit Inc. and Bioptimus, both focusing on pathological images, and by Meta Research Team. We assess variance of embeddings resulting from standard data transformations by comparing original and transformed image embeddings and by contrasting them with random, unrelated embeddings, using image tiles from hematoxylin/eosin-stained sections available in a colorectal tissue dataset and the publicly accessible TCGA dataset.
  Our findings show that embeddings of original and transformed images are closer to each other than to random embeddings, indicating robustness to transformations. However, they are not fully invariant, revealing that the encoder networks do not completely neutralize transformation effects in latent space, explaining why transformation-mediated augmentation of datasets can improve performance. Significant differences were observed between general and histopathology-specific encoder networks.

Abstract: Medical point cloud completion is important for anatomical reconstruction and downstream clinical workflows, yet generative modeling in this setting remains insufficiently studied. PCFM with PTv3 is competitive with the deterministic PTv3 baseline and achieves state-of-the-art generative performance across datasets, while requiring substantially fewer sampling steps than diffusion. At the best operating points, PTv3 also yields clear throughput gains, providing up to a 7$\times$ speed-up for PCFM compared to a PVCNN backbone. S1-Omni-Image supports scientific image understanding, generation, and editing in a unified framework. ### [71] [P-MTP: Efficient Document Parsing via Multi-Token Prediction with Progressive Depth Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24447)
*Le Xiang,Chenxi Zhai,Shu Wei,Jingjing Wu,Qunyi Xie,Xiao Tan,Kunbin Chen,Wei He*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出P-MTP，通过渐进式多token预测与动态草拟，在文档解析中实现高吞吐、低延迟，最高5倍加速且精度几乎不降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLM端到端图到结构化文本虽强，但对token密集型文档推理慢。现有多token预测（MTP）可加速，但在加深look-ahead时训练不稳定，限制速度收益。需要一种稳定可扩展的MTP以提升吞吐并保持精度。

Method: 1) 设计轻量级MTP模块，支持更深look-ahead。2) 提出“渐进式课程损失”：利用累计路径可靠性与回溯目标一致性自适应重加权不同预测深度，抑制长程预测的梯度噪声，实现从易到难的优化过渡。3) 推出“置信门控的动态起草”：推理时按置信度自适应调整推测长度，最大化有效look-ahead与接受率，减少无效计算。

Result: 在多项基准与架构上验证，P-MTP实现最高约5×速度提升，同时精度损失可忽略，首次在文档解析领域成功验证了大深度look-ahead的MTP。

Conclusion: P-MTP通过训练期的渐进式稳定化与推理期的自适应起草，将MTP的look-ahead有效扩展，显著加速文档解析且维持精度，为高吞吐VLM推理提供通用方案。

Abstract: Vision-Language Models (VLMs) have revolutionized document parsing by enabling end-to-end mapping from images to structured text, imposing a significant latency bottleneck, particularly for token-dense documents. While Multi-Token Prediction (MTP) has emerged as a promising approach for accelerating inference, its potential is constrained by optimization instability when scaling to deeper look-ahead depth. In this paper, we propose \textbf{P-MTP}, a framework that leverages \textbf{Progressive Multi-Token Prediction} with a lightweight MTP module to scale the look-ahead depth for high-throughput document parsing. Specifically, we introduce Progressive Curriculum Loss that adaptively re-weights different look-ahead depths using cumulative path reliability and retrospective target consistency. By effectively suppressing gradient noise in long-range predictions, P-MTP, facilitates an automated easy-to-hard optimization transition, enabling the model to master increasingly distant look-ahead depths. Furthermore, we propose Confidence-Gated Dynamic Drafting to maximize the effective look-ahead depth and acceptance rate by adaptively calibrating speculative length during inference, thereby minimizing computational waste and further pushing the boundaries of inference speedup. Experimental results across multiple benchmarks and architectures demonstrate that P-MTP, achieves up to a $5\times$ speedup with negligible loss in accuracy, providing the first successful validation of extensive look-ahead MTP in the document parsing domain.

### [72] [SENTRY: SAM2-Enhanced Neighbor-Aware and Temporally Reasoned Memory for Visual Tracking](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24449)
*Mohamad Alansari,Yonathan Michael,Hasan AlMarzouqi,Muzammal Naseer,Naoufel Werghi,Sajid Javed*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出SENTRY：在SAM2系跟踪器中，将“写入记忆前先验证一致性”的无训练、即插即用模块，替代仅凭置信度的掩码写入，以抑制遮挡、快速运动与干扰物导致的漂移，并在九个基准上获得一致增益与多项零样本SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SAM2系跟踪器的记忆更新通常按掩码置信度直接写入，这在遮挡、快速位移、相似干扰目标场景下易把错误掩码写入记忆，引发持续性漂移。现有评测也未在所有尺度与数据集上统一验证这一问题与改进空间。

Method: 提出SENTRY模块：1) 每帧聚合多样分割假设；2) 将假设回溯成短轨迹片段（短轨迹）；3) 与近期轨迹做邻域感知的循环一致匹配，优先选择在时间与几何上自洽的掩码；4) 仅对通过短时一致性验证的掩码执行写入；无需改动基架构、无需训练；开销约0.4–0.6GB VRAM，SAM2-L在A100上32.8 FPS。

Result: 在五个强基线中集成SENTRY，于九个基准上带来稳定提升；在LaSOT、LaSOT_ext、GOT-10k、VOT20、VOT22、DiDi等实现零样本SOTA；并给出了首次覆盖所有尺度的SAM2系统一评测。

Conclusion: 在记忆写入时强制短时时空一致性，可在不重训、不改主干的前提下稳住记忆增强型跟踪，显著降低漂移并提升跨数据集的稳健性与性能。

Abstract: We revisit the memory update mechanism in SAM2-based visual object tracking and identify confidence-only mask selection as the dominant cause of drift under occlusion, rapid motion, and distractors. We introduce SENTRY, a training-free, plug-and-play, refine-before-write module that validates each memory update for short-horizon temporal consistency before committing it. SENTRY aggregates diverse segmentation hypotheses per frame, backtracks them into short tracklets, and uses neighbor-aware cycle-consistent matching against recent trajectories to favor temporally and geometrically consistent masks. It leaves the base architecture untouched, replacing confidence-driven writes with consistency-validated ones. For fair evaluation, we re-evaluate major open-source SAM2-based trackers across all available scales and datasets, filling gaps in prior reports. Integrated into five strong baselines, SENTRY delivers consistent gains across nine benchmarks, achieving new zero-shot SOTA on LaSOT, LaSOT_ext, GOT-10k, VOT20, VOT22, and DiDi. Despite these checks, the SAM2-L version runs at 32.8 FPS on an A100, and across compatible hosts adds only about 0.4--0.6 GB VRAM. Our results provide the first unified all-scale evaluation of SAM2-based trackers and show that enforcing temporal validity at write time stabilizes memory-augmented tracking without retraining.

In this paper, we challenge this assumption by introducing Lite Any Stereo V2 (LAS2), an ultra-fast model series designed for efficient zero-shot stereo matching. *Yixuan Li,Guangzhi Sun,Yudong Yang,Wei Li,Zejun MA,Chao Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出video-SALMONN-R^3：一种端到端视频LLM，通过强化学习实现“重看”而无需CoT冷启动，结合“再答”“再问”机制，在更低算力成本下显著提升视频QA表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视频LLM受限于算力与显存，通常降低帧率/分辨率，导致关键细节丢失、QA性能下降。现有“先粗看定位、再高保真重看”的范式有效，但多依赖CoT数据与SFT，成本高且可能损伤预训练视频理解能力。需要一种无需CoT、能端到端学会何时与如何重看的方法，并在推理与作答偏好不匹配时保持问答一致性。

Method: - 两阶段但端到端的“重看”框架：先粗看定位相关片段，再以更高时空保真度重看。
- 通过强化学习学习重看策略，无需CoT冷启动与CoT-SFT。
- Re-answer：第一遍先直接给出答案，重看后再基于新证据精炼答案，以缓解预训练模型“先答”偏好与重看“先推理”冲突。
- Re-ask：在重看阶段重新注入问题，提升对问题意图的黏合与检索对齐。
- 端到端训练，优化重看触发、片段选择与最终答案质量。

Result: 在多项视频QA基准上，video-SALMONN-R^3稳健优于基础模型与QA向SFT基线；相较既有重看方法，以显著更低计算成本取得更优或相当性能。

Conclusion: 无需CoT标注与SFT的强化学习重看策略，配合“再答/再问”机制，可在受限算力下有效提升视频LLM的QA效果；该思路兼顾效率与性能，具有实践价值。

Abstract: Video large language models (LLMs) are often constrained by computation and memory budgets, leading them to use reduced frame rates and spatial resolutions, which may cause them to miss critical information for question answering (QA). A practical and efficient solution is a two-stage paradigm: first perform coarse video understanding to localize relevant segments, and then re-watch these segments at higher temporal or spatial fidelity. In this paper, we present video-SALMONN-R$^3$, the first end-to-end video-LLM that enables re-watch through reinforcement learning without relying on chain-of-thought (CoT) cold-start. This design removes the need for costly CoT data annotations and avoids CoT-based supervised fine-tuning (SFT), which can otherwise degrade the pretrained video understanding abilities. To address the mismatch between the reasoning-first behavior induced by re-watch and the answer-first tendency of pretrained video-LLMs, we propose a re-answer strategy, in which the model first produces a direct answer in the first watch and then refines it after re-watching. Finally, to improve question adherence during re-watching, we propose a re-ask mechanism that re-injects the query when revisiting localized segments. Experimental results show that video-SALMONN-R$^3$ consistently outperforms both the base model and the QA-SFT baseline, while surpassing prior re-watch-based approaches with significantly lower computational cost. Code, models, and data will be publicly released upon acceptance.

</details>


### [76] [MambaRaw: Selective State Space Modeling for Efficient 4K Raw Image Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24479)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于元数据的原始图像重建虽可利用机内JPEG参考，但其上下文/注意力模型在高分辨率（如4K）时计算与内存开销大（注意力随特征图二次增长），限制了实际应用。

Method: 构建JPEG条件的元数据压缩-重建框架MambaRaw，以状态空间模型（SSM）高效估计熵参数。核心是“空间-能量耦合上下文建模”：1) TileMambaBlock：仅在信息密集的图像瓦片上进行Mamba式选择性扫描，降低时空建模成本并聚焦有效上下文；2) Energy-Aware Refinement (EAR)：以恒等初始化的残差模块，增强特征表达以适配原始信号长尾能量分布。

Result: 在Sony、Olympus、Samsung三数据集上，较强基线持续提升并达SOTA；在低元数据码率条件下，PSNR提升1.2–1.4 dB，端到端编码时延约降9%。

Conclusion: 通过SSM驱动的空间-能量耦合上下文与轻量模块，MambaRaw在计算效率与重建质量间取得更优权衡，适用于高分辨率原始图像的JPEG引导重建，并具备实际部署价值。

Abstract: In-camera JPEG previews are ubiquitous in raw image formats and provide an sRGB reference at negligible storage cost. Although existing metadata-based reconstruction frameworks can exploit this side information when recovering raw images, their context models often become computationally expensive especially at high resolution, eg, 4K raw image, given that attention mechanisms scale quadratically with feature maps, hindering its practical application. To address these limitations, we propose MambaRaw, a JPEG-conditioned metadata-based raw image reconstruction framework that uses State Space Models (SSMs) to estimate entropy parameters efficiently. Our key contribution comprises a Spatial-Energy Coupled Context Modeling mechanism with two lightweight modules: (1) TileMambaBlock, which performs Mamba-style selective scanning only on information-dense tiles to improve the efficiency; and (2) Energy-Aware Refinement (EAR), an identity-initialized residual module that enhance feature representation to match the long-tail energy distribution of raw signals. Extensive experiments on three camera datasets (Sony, Olympus, Samsung) show consistent improvements over strong metadata-based baselines and set a new state of the art for JPEG-guided raw reconstruction with great efficiency. Notably, at low metadata bitrates, MambaRaw increases PSNR by 1.2--1.4 dB and reduces end-to-end coding latency by about 9%. Code is released at https://github.com/Peizeli1/MambaRaw.

### [78] [RetiSEM: Generalising Causal Models for Fragmented Biomedical Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24488)
*Inam Ullah,Imran Razzak,Shoaib Jameel*

Main category: cs.CV

Abstract: Learning causal models from fragmented biomedical data is challenging because clinical, molecular, and imaging variables are often incomplete or not jointly observed. We propose RetiSEM, a domain-constrained structural equation modelling (SEM) framework for causal graph recovery and mediation analysis under limited multimodal resources. This proposed work organises variables into biologically informed blocks, applies forbidden-edge constraints, and decomposes pathway-level effects into TE, NDE, and NIE components. We evaluate RetiSEM across ten synthetic benchmark scenarios that vary in dimensionality, nonlinearity, causal depth, and pathway structure, together with a fragmented real-world setting that combines NHANES clinical variables with externally derived retinal representations. This approach achieves lower structural error and higher causal accuracy than unconstrained baselines across the synthetic benchmarks. In the real-data analysis, retinal variables behave mainly as downstream biomarker-like indicators, with smaller but detectable indirect effects. These findings support our strategy as an interpretable framework for testing structured causal hypotheses in limited-resource biomedical AI. The code and resources for this work are publicly available at: https://github.com/Inamullah-Colab/ReitSEM.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer在全局注意力下易忽略微小几何关系，导致手指指向射线捕捉不准，远距或密集目标时产生漂移与歧义，影响AR与人机协作中的空间交互。

Method: 1) LHEM：将手部姿态/关键点嵌入为局部实体特征，强化对细微手指偏转的感知；2) GRM：受多视几何启发，将隐式方向信息显式化为空间几何射线特征，用于引导特征聚合与深度融合的注意力；3) OCAL损失：联合监督手部存在性与指向一致性，使网络朝着空间定位核心目标优化。

Result: 在指向落点定位任务上，相比基线取得约14点绝对精度提升；定性结果显示从手到目标的几何关联建模更稳健，缓解传统Transformer的空间感知缺陷。

Abstract: Grounding deictic gestures in natural images is fundamental to AR and human-robot collaboration, providing a basis for seamless spatial interaction. While Transformer-based visual models have achieved significant progress in general object detection, their global attention mechanisms often neglect micro-geometric relationships, degrading orientation accuracy. In pointing tasks, this deficiency manifests as an inability to accurately capture the pointing ray implied by finger poses, which results in pointing drift and localization ambiguity when dealing with distant or densely packed objects. To address this, we propose VistaRef, a framework designed to explicitly enhance spatial orientation awareness. First, we develop the Local Hand Entity Modeling (LHEM) module, which incorporates hand-pose embeddings to strengthen the model's capability to capture subtle finger deviations. Second, drawing inspiration from multi-view geometry, we construct the Geometric Ray Modeling (GRM) module to transform implicit orientation information into explicit spatial geometric features, guiding feature aggregation and deep fusion via attention mechanisms. Furthermore, we introduce a novel Orientation-Consistent Alignment Loss (OCAL) to synergistically supervise hand presence and pointing consistency, ensuring that all architectural improvements collectively serve the core objective of spatial localization. Experimental results demonstrate that VistaRef significantly outperforms the baseline, achieving a 14-point absolute gain in grounding accuracy. Qualitative analysis further confirms that VistaRef effectively models the geometric correlation from hand to target, bridging the spatial perception gap inherent in traditional Transformers for complex scenarios. Code: https://github.com/lingli1724/VistaRef.

### [80] [GeoIMO: Geometry-Driven Independent Motion Classification for Event Cameras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24499)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有汽车事件数据集的标注多来自帧相机外观信息，难以用于基于运动的事件感知研究；需要一种不依赖外观标注、能直接从事件流中区分静止与独立运动目标的方法。

Method: 1) 直接从事件流估计自运动：采用带偏航补偿的膨胀焦点（FOE）模型拟合全局背景运动；2) 对每个检测到的目标，比较其局部事件运动与全局预测的差异；3) 以尺度不变残差度量偏离程度并判为“独立运动”；4) 跨连续事件窗口进行时间稳定化以提升鲁棒性；5) 方法无需学习、无需手动运动标签，可接收任意来源的检测框输入。

Conclusion: 几何驱动、无监督（无标注/无训练）的事件相机运动分离框架可稳健地区分静止与独立运动目标，具有泛化性强、工程落地成本低的优势，尤其在车辆转向场景中受益于偏航补偿；简单的局部平移建模已足够实用。

Abstract: Existing automotive event datasets rely on appearance-based annotations from frame pipelines, making them poorly suited for motion-aware event perception. We present a geometry-driven, annotation-free framework that classifies detected objects as static or independently moving by exploiting ego-motion structure directly from the event stream. A Focus of Expansion model with yaw compensation estimates global background motion, while objects are labeled as moving when local motion deviates from this prediction, as quantified by a scale-invariant residual. Temporal stabilization improves robustness across consecutive event windows. The method requires no learning, no manual motion labels, and works with any input bounding boxes. Experiments on MVSEC and the Prophesee 1 Megapixel Automotive Detection dataset demonstrate consistent performance across diverse driving scenarios, with yaw compensation improving results during turns and a simple translational local model offering a favorable accuracy-efficiency trade-off.

### [81] [What Do Flow-Based Inverse Solvers Approximate? A Posterior-Transport View](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24516)
*Jian Xu,Delu Zeng,John Paisley,Qibin Zhao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 论文提出对基于flow-matching先验的“无训练”逆问题求解器（FlowDPS/FLOWER/PnP-Flow等）的统一后验传输视角，指出对确定性flow先验，严格的贝叶斯条件化应通过源分布重加权并沿未修改的速度场推送即可得到精确后验；现有逐步测量引导其实是在逼近一个最小动能校正场，并由此带来可量化的后验偏差。作者给出理论界限、2D可控实验验证，并提出一种廉价且更原则的速度校正求解器，兼具精度与不确定性表达。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于概率流/扩散先验的逆问题方法常通过在ODE中加入测量引导项实现“训练外”求解，虽效果好，但缺乏对其近似对象与与真实后验偏差的系统刻画；需要澄清：这些校正在理论上对应什么？与真正的后验采样有多远？能否据此设计更原则的求解器。

Method: 1) 提出“后验传输”框架：对确定性flow prior，后验等价于对源分布的重加权并通过原始速度场传输；2) 将轨迹引导视为将无条件源转变为后验所需的最小动能校正场，并解析FlowDPS/FLOWER/PnP-Flow分别是该校正的零阶/高斯/近端近似；3) 给出Wasserstein距离上的后验偏差上界；4) 在有闭式后验的2D受控设定中实证比较；5) 依据分析提出廉价的速度校正求解器，并在AFHQ、CelebA及OOD设定上评测。

Result: 理论上：证明源重加权+未改速度场可产生精确后验；刻画并上界了轨迹引导法的后验偏差。实证上：2D实验中，源重加权达到了蒙特卡洛下限，而轨迹引导误差大200–800倍并出现模态塌缩，且与引导强度无关；新提出的速度校正解法在两类域内先验与两类OOD任务上具竞争力，并能产生多样化样本且不确定性与重建误差正相关。

Conclusion: 对确定性flow先验，正确的贝叶斯条件化应通过源分布重加权而非在流场中加入漂移修正；现有FlowDPS/FLOWER/PnP-Flow只是最小动能校正场的不同近似，导致可量化的后验偏差与模态塌缩。基于该视角的新速度校正求解器在保持训练自由的同时改进了后验质量与不确定性表征。

Abstract: A growing family of training-free solvers -- FlowDPS, FLOWER, PnP-Flow and their diffusion ancestors (DPS, DAPS) -- repurpose a pretrained flow-matching prior to solve imaging inverse problems by adding a measurement-guidance term to the deterministic probability-flow ODE. Despite strong empirical results, what these per-step corrections actually approximate -- and how far the resulting samples are from the true posterior $p(x\mid y)$ -- has not been characterized. We give a posterior-transport account of flow-based inverse problem solving. Our starting point is a simple but consequential fact: for a \emph{deterministic} flow prior, Bayesian conditioning is realized entirely by a \emph{reweighting of the source distribution}, not by a drift correction; pushing the reweighted source through the \emph{unmodified} velocity field yields exact posterior samples. From this we show that trajectory-guidance solvers can be read as the minimum-kinetic-energy \emph{correction} field needed to morph the unconditional source into the posterior, and that FlowDPS / FLOWER / PnP-Flow correspond to distinct zeroth-order / Gaussian / proximal approximations of this single object; we bound the resulting posterior bias in Wasserstein distance. A controlled $2$D study with a closed-form posterior confirms the theory decisively: source reweighting matches the true posterior to the Monte-Carlo floor on every metric, whereas trajectory guidance incurs $200$--$800\times$ larger error and collapses posterior modes, \emph{regardless of guidance strength}. Guided by the analysis we propose a cheap, principled velocity-correction solver that is competitive across two in-domain priors (AFHQ, CelebA) and two out-of-distribution settings while, unlike point-estimate source-space optimizers, producing diverse posterior samples with uncertainty that correlates with reconstruction error.

</details>


### [82] [VisCritic: Visual State Comparison as Process Reward for GUI Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24525)
*Jiachen Qian*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: VisCritic：以视觉对比为核心的GUI代理过程奖励框架。通过Siamese ViT对前后截图抽取变化感知特征，并由动作感知评估头联合判定动作是否成功、任务进展与错误类型；利用无人工标注的弱监督数据构建流程进行训练；在五个基准上作为即插即用组件提升多类GUI代理表现并提供可视诊断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有GUI代理在长程任务易失败，关键原因是缺乏逐步验证；已有过程奖励多仅凭文本推理，忽视GUI状态变化的视觉本质，需要一种能直接利用界面视觉差异来判别动作效果与进展的机制。

Method: 提出VisCritic：1) Siamese视觉Transformer对动作前/后截图编码，获得对变化敏感的表示；2) 动作感知评估头联合预测动作成功、任务进度增益与错误类型；3) 通过从现有轨迹自动合成弱监督训练样本的管线，无需额外人工标注；4) 以插件形式为多种GUI代理提供视觉过程奖励与诊断。

Result: 在五个基准与离线分析中，VisCritic作为插件普遍提升指标（成功率/效率等），并能输出可解释的视觉诊断线索；对多类GUI代理均有效。

Conclusion: 直接对比前后截图的视觉过程奖励能更可靠地验证动作并指引长程任务执行；VisCritic在无需额外人工标注的前提下提升通用GUI代理表现，且具备可解释诊断价值。

Abstract: GUI agents powered by vision-language models show strong potential for automating digital tasks, yet frequently fail in long-horizon scenarios due to the absence of step-level verification. Existing process reward models verify actions through textual reasoning alone, missing the visual nature of GUI state changes. We introduce VisCritic, a visual process reward framework that verifies agent actions by directly comparing pre-action and post-action screenshots in visual feature space. VisCritic employs a Siamese vision transformer to extract change-aware representations, coupled with an Action-Aware Critic Head that jointly evaluates action success, task progress, and error type. A critic-training data construction pipeline generates weakly supervised samples from existing trajectories without additional human labels for critic training. Experiments and offline analyses across five benchmarks demonstrate that VisCritic serves as a plug-and-play enhancement for diverse GUI agents, generally improving benchmark metrics while providing visual diagnostic cues.

Method: 1) 把篡改定位表述为自回归序列生成，直接生成空间对齐的token序列。2) Token Splatting Decoder（TSD）：基于码本感知的code smoothing，将token映射为二值掩码，缓解确定性去token化带来的尖锐梯度。3) Hierarchical Expert Fusion（HEF）：将取证专家模型的多尺度特征注入MLLM，实现分层融合，补足通用MLLM缺乏的取证先验。统一架构端到端训练，无中间监督。

ForensicsTok directly generates spatially grounded token sequences, enabling precise mask prediction without intermediary supervision. Furthermore, to capture diverse tampering clues, we propose a Hierarchical Expert Fusion (HEF) module that injects multi-scale features from a forensic expert model. ### [85] [Are Text-to-Image Models Inductivist Turkeys? A Counterfactual Benchmark for Causal Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.24548)
*Jiayi Lei,Yuandong Pu,Xingyu Han,Rongpeng Zhu,Jing Xu,Jinyao Wang,Zijian Zhou,Bin Fu,Yuewen Cao,Yihao Liu,Yongsheng Li*

Method: 构建CF-World，将每个场景分三层：1) 事实生成（普通常识）；2) 显式反事实（给出直接视觉指令）；3) 隐式反事实（需基于改写规则进行因果推断）。使用VLM评测器CF-Eval进行自动评价，并提出两项指标：PRR衡量抵抗现实先验能力，RRR衡量在无显式提示下保持反事实推理生成的能力。评测开源与闭源T2I模型。

Conclusion: 当前T2I主要依赖视觉-文本共现的模式匹配而非稳健的因果推理。要提升反事实生成与规则遵循，应弱化对共现先验的依赖并增强可组合、可更新的规则与因果表征与推理能力。

Abstract: Text-to-image (T2I) generation models have achieved remarkable progress in producing visually realistic images from natural language prompts. Yet it remains unclear whether their success reflects genuine causal understanding or sophisticated pattern matching over visual-textual correlations. Inspired by Russell's inductivist turkey, we introduce Counterfactual-World (CF-World), a counterfactual benchmark designed to investigate whether text-to-image models can generate images under rules that systematically contradict real-world priors. CF-World organizes each scenario into three progressive levels: factual generation under ordinary world knowledge, explicit counterfactual generation with direct visual instructions, and implicit counterfactual generation requiring causal deduction from altered rules. We evaluate both open-source and closed-source T2I models using a Vision Language Model (VLM)-based evaluator (CF-Eval). Furthermore, we introduce two metrics: Prior Resistance Rate (PRR), which measures a model's ability to overcome entrenched real-world priors, and Reasoning Retention Rate (RRR), which assesses whether models can maintain reasoning-dependent counterfactual generation without explicit visual cues. Experiments show that all models exhibit sharp degradation from factual to counterfactual settings. Further analyses suggest that these failures arise because current T2I models encode world knowledge and visual appearances as tightly coupled patterns. Consequently, their heavy reliance on frequent visual co-occurrences within the training data forces them to default to familiar commonsense priors when tasked with rendering counterfactual worlds.
